-   [<span data-ttu-id="31b43-107">事务集 CNTCND CONAPW</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="31b43-107">Transaction Sets CNTCND-CONAPW</span></span>](../core/edifact-transaction-sets-aperak-iftrin.md#cntcnd)

-   [<span data-ttu-id="31b43-110">事务集 CUSCAR DEBREC</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="31b43-110">Transaction Sets CUSCAR-DEBREC</span></span>](../core/edifact-transaction-sets-aperak-iftrin.md#cuscar)
